There are two ways for you to do that:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>Key-in the appropriate search term for the product or item that you want in the search bar that says “search for products, coupons, or brands…” found on top most part of the home page. After typing it in simply hit the enter button on your keyboard or the magnifying glass button on the rightmost part of the search bar.</li>\n<li>At the home page, you will immediately see different product categories, they’re divided into three (3) main categories and hundreds of sub-categories. The three (3) main categories are Electronics &amp; Gaming, Fashion &amp; Beauty, and Coupon &amp; Offers. Upon clicking on these main categories, it will scroll down its respective subcategories, by clicking on those, you will be instantly taken to a list of products from the subcategory which you think best fits the product that you want. Scroll through the products page until you’ve found what you are looking for.</li>\n</ul>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Compare prices from different stores!</strong></h3>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The compare feature of iPrice Singapore lets you find the best offers for your chosen products among the most reliable shops on the internet in a single page.
